\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
This is a general header that includes C language support.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SDL\_abs()}{SDL\_abs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_aa4c7a931f4a968f818b2a1b10a432185}{DECLSPEC}} int \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_a81faf4ba0455dc75f2e0507eddb79401}{SDLCALL}} SDL\+\_\+abs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{x }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_aad4335bccd2da5d4cbc56227a00c5e6a}\label{_s_d_l__stdinc_8h_aad4335bccd2da5d4cbc56227a00c5e6a}} 
\index{SDL\_stdinc.h@{SDL\_stdinc.h}!SDL\_acos@{SDL\_acos}}
\index{SDL\_acos@{SDL\_acos}!SDL\_stdinc.h@{SDL\_stdinc.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{SDL\_acos()}{SDL\_acos()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_aa4c7a931f4a968f818b2a1b10a432185}{DECLSPEC}} double \mbox{\hyperlink{begin__code_8h_a81faf4ba0455dc75f2e0507eddb79401}{SDLCALL}} SDL\+\_\+acos (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{double}]{x }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Use this function to compute arc cosine of {\ttfamily x}.

The definition of {\ttfamily y = acos(x)} is {\ttfamily x = cos(y)}.

Domain\+: {\ttfamily -\/1 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= x \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= 1}

Range\+: {\ttfamily 0 \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= y \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}= Pi}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em x} & floating point value, in radians. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
arc cosine of {\ttfamily x}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
This function is available since SDL 2.\+0.\+2. 
\end{DoxySince}
